Sourceshared.css
AnatomySticky header (back + title/sub + save status) with a built-in Header shadow via the .edge-shadow utility (token var(--shadow-header), shown only below — inset, tapered, no bottom border; see Pillar 1 · 1.5 Shadow) + body content + sticky bottom action bar.
Behavior / usageDraft / back-next / review; no global topbar. Header shadow separates the sticky header from scrolling content (ref. Figma 720:1763). 2026-07-16: the top-left back arrow (.wizard__back) and title block (.wizard__top-titlewrap) merge into a single back button — .wizard__top-lead is a pill surface that fills with --accent on hover (--radius-lg 8px, padding 8/16/8/8, ref. Figma 781:4142); clicking the title also goes back. The real button stays the inner .wizard__back, whose stretched ::after (inset:0) extends the hit-area and focus ring over the whole lead — no consumer-page markup change. 2026-07-24: the header's three tracks are minmax(var(--wizard-lead-min), 1fr) minmax(0, 820px) minmax(min-content, 1fr) — the left track gets a 180px floor. With two plain 1fr sides the title block (min-width:0 + ellipsis) could shrink to 0 while the right side could not, so a narrow viewport collapsed the left track and the title overflowed onto the stepper; the floor makes the stepper absorb the squeeze instead. Wide layouts are unchanged.
Token usage--card, --border, --shadow-micro, display type.

Evidence / usagecreate-project · create-product · create-event.

4.52b Stock bar

🟢 atom

Purpose

用途

A 5px horizontal quantity bar that says "how much is left" at a glance — stock level, usage ratio. Always pairs with the exact figure next to it (e.g. "3 / 50"): the bar carries the feel, the number carries the truth, and neither substitutes for the other. Thinner and simpler than the Completeness meter, which owns its own label + count header; this one is bare track + fill and expects the surrounding card to supply the wording.

5px 高的水平量條，一眼讀出「還剩多少」——庫存水位、用量比例。一定要搭配旁邊的精確數字（例如「3 / 50」）：量條負責體感、數字負責精確值，兩者不可互相取代。比 Completeness meter 更細更簡單——那支自帶標籤＋計數表頭，本元件只有軌道＋填充，文字由外層的卡提供。

Relationships

元件關係

Built from由哪些元件組成 ↓
Self-contained — no nested components自成一體 — 無嵌套其他元件
Used by被哪些元件使用 ↑
organismDetail rail

Rendered preview (both states — normal fill, and --low below the low-stock threshold)

視覺展示 (兩種狀態——正常填充，以及低於低庫存門檻的 --low)

In stock庫存31 / 50
In stock庫存3 / 50

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Pass the percentage as an inline style="width:N%" on .stock-bar__fill — it is data, not styling, so it belongs to the consumer page, and the component sets no width of its own.
  • 百分比用 inline style="width:N%" 寫在 .stock-bar__fill 上——那是資料不是樣式，屬於 consumer 頁；元件本身不預設寬度。
  • Always show the exact figure alongside the bar.
  • 量條旁一定要顯示精確數字。
Don't別做
  • Don't invent a third colour. The bar has exactly two states — normal and --low; anything finer is a product rule.
  • 別自創第三種顏色。量條只有兩態——正常與 --low；再細的分級屬於產品規則。
  • Don't decide the low threshold in CSS — where "low" begins is a product rule the consumer evaluates before adding the modifier.
  • 別在 CSS 裡決定低庫存門檻——「多低算低」是產品規則，由 consumer 判斷後才加上修飾子。
For developers — classes · code給工程師 — class · 程式碼
.stock-barTrack — 5px tall, --muted fill, --radius-pill, overflow:hidden, --sp-8 vertical margin軌道——5px 高、--muted 底、--radius-pill、overflow:hidden、--sp-8 上下外距
.stock-bar__fillFill — --primary, full height; width comes from the consumer's inline style填充——--primary、滿高；寬度由 consumer 的 inline style 提供
.stock-bar__fill--lowBelow the low-stock threshold — fill switches to --destructive低於低庫存門檻——填充改 --destructive

Token usageToken 使用: --muted · --primary · --destructive · --radius-pill · --sp-8

Consumers採用頁: product-detail.html (right-rail "current stock" card)(右欄「當前庫存」卡)

ds-components/stock-bar.css

4.53 Store settings page

🟠 organism

Purpose

用途

E-Shop store-level settings as a popup (store-settings.html, spec 5.1.5.5 / D035 / D067) opened from E-Shop F3 as an embed-modal iframe — no global nav / breadcrumb / page header (the modal frame owns the title + close); actions sit in a bottom submit bar (.ss-actionbar). IA: a persistent Storefront card on top — a Base44 / Facebook-style identity band (cover + overlapping logo avatar + shop name / URL / bio shown as text) with per-field click-to-edit in place (.ss-edit: read text ↔ inline input/textarea/select, ✓/Enter commits, ✕/Esc cancels). Brand assets are the cover + avatar (edited via their own buttons) — no separate upload tiles. Then three peer setting groups (Product display / Payment / Shipping) as tabs (one at a time), plus a See as fan split preview. The whole page fills the standard 1280px .page column like other pages (it is not a two-column detail page, so it does not take .page--narrow). This component adds the field types base controls don't cover — URL affix (.ss-url), $ amount affix (.amount-field), read-only Stripe card (.ss-status) — the drag-to-reorder list (.ss-order, fan-side order · F3 / D031) and the fan preview body (.ss-fan).

電子商店「商店層級設定」popup（store-settings.html，spec 5.1.5.5 / D035 / D067），由 E-Shop F3 以 embed-modal iframe 開啟——無全域導航／麵包屑／頁首（標題與關閉由 modal 外框提供），動作置底部提交列（.ss-actionbar）。IA：店面門面卡常駐置頂——用 Base44／Facebook 式身分帶（封面＋疊加 logo 頭像＋店名／網址／簡介為文字），逐欄就地編輯（.ss-edit：文字態 ↔ 內嵌 input/textarea/select，✓/Enter 確認、✕/Esc 取消）。品牌素材就是封面＋頭像（各自有編輯鈕），不另設上傳框——其下商品陳列／付款／出貨三個對等設定群組以 tab 切換（一次處理其一），另有 粉絲視角預覽（See as fan）畫面分割。整頁用滿標準 1280px 的 .page 欄寬（非兩欄詳情頁，不套 .page--narrow）。本元件補基礎控制項沒有的欄位型別——網址前綴（.ss-url）、金額前綴（.amount-field）、唯讀 Stripe 卡（.ss-status）——拖曳排序清單（.ss-order，粉絲端順序 · F3 / D031）與粉絲預覽內容（.ss-fan）。

4.55 Preview column

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

The "form | preview" two-column layout for create flows: a left form column and a right sticky preview column (title + grey sub + live preview content). Replaces the old slide-out Preview panel; the card inside reuses Preview card. Every box inside the column (Preview card, Listing settings card) drops its 1px border and takes the floating-card treatment instead, so the right column matches the left column's form-section --outlined (2026-07-21). Used by create-product, create-bundle, create-auction and create-campaign.

建立流程的「表單｜預覽」兩欄版面：左表單、右一條 sticky 預覽欄（標題＋灰副標＋即時預覽）。取代舊滑出式 Preview panel；欄內的卡重用 Preview card。欄內所有盒子（預覽卡、上架設定卡）都去掉 1px 邊框、改用浮起卡的填色＋陰影＋上緣光，與左欄的 form-section --outlined 一致（2026-07-21）。create-product、create-bundle、create-auction、create-campaign 使用。

4.56 Preview panel

🟠 organism

Right-hand split panel holding the live preview card (spec §5.2.5) — not an overlay. Opened on demand by the create-flow top-bar Preview button: it takes layout on the right and compresses the wizard (body.preview-open), so the form stays visible and editable; no dim scrim. ✕ / Esc closes and restores. Shown here statically.

右側畫面分割面板，承載即時預覽卡（規格 §5.2.5）——非浮層遮蓋。由建立流程頂部 Preview 鈕按需開啟：佔版面、把 wizard 壓窄（body.preview-open），表單仍可見可編輯，無變暗遮罩。✕／Esc 關閉復位。此處靜態展示。

Reused by E-Shop F5 “Store preview” (5.1.5): .preview-panel--inset compresses .main instead of the wizard. There it is toggleable, default-closed (opened from the F3 “Store preview” button; closed via a floating ✕ in the sheet’s top-right + Esc — spec F5 / D084) and runs headerless (no .preview-panel__head; the “商店預覽” label lives in the fan-store hero overline). On narrow screens (≤1100px) it falls back to a static block stacked below the list.

由 E-Shop F5「商店預覽」（5.1.5）重用：.preview-panel--inset 壓窄的是 .main 而非 wizard。在該頁為可開關、預設關閉（由 F3「商店預覽」鈕開啟；關閉走 sheet 右上浮動 ✕＋Esc——spec F5／D084），且為 headerless（無 .preview-panel__head，「商店預覽」標題移進 fan-store hero overline）。窄螢幕（≤1100px）退化為靜態區塊堆疊在清單下方。

4.57 Fan store preview

🟠 organism

The fan-side storefront rendered inside every “See as fan” preview — shared by E-Shop F5 (Store preview) and Store settings F1. Per spec §6.7 the preview is the fan end (same source, difference = defect), so both pages inject one shared markup (partials/fan-store.js). 2026-07-02: presented as a mobile phone — a dark device shell (.fan-store__phone) whose self-scrolling screen (.fan-store__screen) is the fan-app store page: app bar (menu · ztor. · cart/user) + hero (artist name over a dark gradient cover + socials + Join community) + sticky app-section pills (Shop/Events/Ranks/Posts/About) + featured + Products/Bundles/Auctions underline sub-tabs + 2-col product grid with cart buttons + Top fans + About + sticky bottom app nav. Layout direction from the endgame creator-store mobile prototype (visual evidence only).

每個「See as fan」預覽內呈現的粉絲端店面，由 E-Shop F5（商店預覽）與 商店設定 F1 共用。依規格 §6.7，預覽＝粉絲端（同源、差異即缺陷），兩頁注入同一份 markup（partials/fan-store.js）。2026-07-02 改為手機呈現——深色手機外殼（.fan-store__phone）內的自捲動螢幕（.fan-store__screen）即粉絲 app 商店頁：app 頂列（menu · ztor. · 購物車/帳號）＋hero（名字壓深色漸層封面＋社群＋加入社群）＋sticky app 分頁列（商店/活動/排行榜/貼文/關於）＋本月精選＋商品/組合/拍賣底線子分頁＋雙欄商品格（含購物車圓鈕）＋頭號粉絲＋關於＋sticky 底部 app 導航。版型方向取自 endgame creator 商店手機版原型（僅視覺證據）。

⚠ Theme exception: the phone screen is the fan app's fixed-dark surface (theme-independent, like the VIP-card art) — dark neutrals are scoped --fst-* custom props; brand orange stays var(--primary). See “Raw-color exceptions” in design-system.md.

⚠ 主題例外：手機螢幕是粉絲 app 的固定深色面（不跟隨後台主題，同 VIP 卡面前例）——深色中性色為 scoped --fst-* custom props；品牌橘仍用 var(--primary)。見 design-system.md「Raw-color exceptions」。

⚠ Followers count, social links (YT/IG/TH/X), Join community, featured, Buy now, “sold out · restocking”, app section pills (Events/Ranks/Posts/About), Top fans, About-the-creator, cart buttons and the bottom app nav are product-change proposals pending upstream (ASSUMPTIONS UIA-026) — shown as proposal presentation, not yet written into documents/.

⚠ 追蹤數、社群連結（YT/IG/TH/X）、加入社群、本月精選、立即購買、「售完補貨中」、app 分頁列（活動/排行榜/貼文/關於）、頭號粉絲、關於創作者、購物車鈕與底部 app 導航為產品變更提案，待上游核准（ASSUMPTIONS UIA-026）——以提案呈現，尚未寫回 documents/。

4.58 Dropdown menu

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

Native <details>/<summary> action menu: any .btn as trigger, a floating panel of action links below-right. No JS — open/close is the native details toggle. Use for "create / more actions" menus in toolbars; avoid for nav mega-dropdowns (use NavigationMenu) and for form value selection (use a select/Input).

原生 <details>/<summary> 動作選單：任一 .btn 當觸發器，下方靠右浮出動作連結面板。不需 JS — 開合走原生 details。用於工具列的「建立／更多動作」選單；導覽 mega-dropdown 別用（改用 NavigationMenu），表單選值也別用（改用 select／Input）。

Relationships

元件關係

Built from由哪些元件組成 ↓
atomButton

Rendered preview (open state pinned for display)

視覺展示 (展示用固定展開)

＋ New ▾
Create new product Create bundle from products Create auction
Edit

Triggers: any .btn (primary ＋ New or a btn--icon kebab for per-row actions). Items can be <a> (navigate) or <button> (run JS — reset to look like a link); state-dependent items toggle with [hidden] (e.g. E-Shop row publish/unpublish). E-Shop product rows use the kebab variant; native <details> needs page JS for outside-click / select-to-close.

觸發器：任何 .btn（主要 ＋ New，或列操作用 btn--icon kebab）。選單項可用 <a>（導頁）或 <button>（跑 JS，已重置成連結外觀）；隨狀態切換的選單項用 [hidden] 互斥顯示（如電子商店列的上架/下架）。電子商店商品列用 kebab 變體；原生 <details> 的「點外部／選後收起」需頁面 JS 補。

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Use a real .btn variant as the summary trigger.
  • 用真正的 .btn 變體當 summary 觸發器。
  • Keep items short, action-first, max ~6 entries.
  • 項目精短、動詞開頭，最多約 6 條。
  • Lead every item with a matching .ztor-icon (2026-07-21 使用者裁示) — the only exception is .dropdown__item--toggle (a switch row, e.g. E-Shop's List-in-shop toggle).
  • 每個選項前面都要有對應的 .ztor-icon（2026-07-21 使用者裁示）——唯一例外是 .dropdown__item--toggle（開關列，如電子商店的「在商店上架」）。
Don't別做
  • Don't rebuild it per page with inline styles — link dropdown-menu.css.
  • 別在頁內用 inline style 重刻 — 連結 dropdown-menu.css。
  • Don't use it for navigation menus or form selects.
  • 別拿來做導覽選單或表單下拉選值。

4.60 View switch ✝ retired

⚰️ tombstone

Retired 2026-07-23. A pill-shaped two-icon toggle (solid foreground fill on the active side) that flipped Projects between list and card view. User feedback: it read as ugly and off-system — the solid fill was a third way of drawing "selected" on this site, fighting Segmented control's white-raised pill. Its role — switching the view of the same data — is what Segmented control already owns, so it was folded into that component's icon-only variant .segmented__btn--icon rather than kept as a second pattern. Rules removed from shared.css (tombstone comment left in place).

2026-07-23 退場。膠囊形雙圖示切換器（選中側實心填 foreground），原本用於 Projects 的清單／卡片切換。使用者反饋很醜、和 design system 不搭——實心填是站上第三種「已選中」畫法，與 Segmented control 的白浮起 pill 打架。它的角色（同一資料的視角切換）本來就屬於 Segmented control，因此收斂成該元件的純圖示變體 .segmented__btn--icon，不另留第二套。規則已自 shared.css 移除（原處留墓碑註解）。

4.61 Payout bank picker & dialog

🟠 organism

Purpose

用途

Two-part payout flow (spec §5.1.8): a page-side bank picker card grid (.payout-bank-*) on the Earnings · Payouts tab, plus the request-payout modal (.payout-modal backdrop + .payout-dialog shell with head / body / foot, amount input, summary and success view). Mounted from partials/payout-request-modal.js on earnings.html; the same dialog shell is reused by the F10 manual-entry modal (partials/manual-entry-modal.js).

兩段式撥款流程（spec §5.1.8）：Earnings · Payouts 分頁的頁面側銀行挑選卡格（.payout-bank-*），加上請款 modal（.payout-modal 背板＋.payout-dialog 外殼，含 head／body／foot、金額輸入、摘要與成功畫面）。由 partials/payout-request-modal.js 掛載；目前唯一 consumer 是 earnings.html。

4.62 Restock table

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

Restock popup for the E-Shop restock sub-flow (spec §5.1.5.6, D104 order model + D106 member tabs). A restock is one order: the popup reuses the canonical payout dialog shell (.payout-modal / .payout-dialog) with a document layer — method as .segmented.radio-cards (two side-by-side cards + top-right orange dot, Restock now / Scheduled) plus supplier / notes and, for Scheduled, an expected-arrival date — and an item layer that is a .restock-table of three number columns per row: Current (read-only), Restock (typeable), After (read-only, live current + restock). 2026-07-22 layout (Figma node 861-28842): the item table sits right below the method (product-name label then table); supplier / notes / ETA move below the table; the footer (Cancel / Submit) is pinned to the dialog bottom — only the body scrolls (same pattern as the platform-fee modal); the old under-method hint row and the yellow stickynote have been removed. A product's variants are a matrix of rows (single-variant = 1 row; 2-option = sub-grouped by option-1 via .restock-table__group) — no tabs. A bundle separates its member products with .tabs (one tab per member); each tab panel (.tab-panel) holds that member's variant table. Only one tab level (members) — variants never use tabs; quantities persist across tabs. History log on product-detail reuses .data-list. Mounted from partials/restock-modal.js.

E-Shop 補貨子流程 popup（spec §5.1.5.6，D104 補貨單＋D106 成員 tab）。一次補貨＝一張補貨單：popup 重用 canonical payout dialog 外殼（.payout-modal／.payout-dialog），單據層＝補貨方式改用 .segmented.radio-cards（兩張並排卡＋右上橘點，立即／定時）＋供應商／備註，定時另加預計到貨時間，整張填一次；品項層＝.restock-table 三欄數字表，每列：當前數量（唯讀）、補貨數量（可填）、補後數量（唯讀，即時＝當前＋補貨）。2026-07-22 版型（Figma node 861-28842）：逐選項表移到方式正下方（先商品名稱標題再表格）；供應商／備註／預計到貨改到表格下方；footer（取消／送出補貨）釘在框底、只捲 body（與平台費率彈窗同一套）；方式下方的灰色提示行與底部黃色 stickynote 已移除。商品的規格是矩陣列（單一選項＝1 列；2 選項以選項一分組 .restock-table__group）——不用 tab。組合則以 .tabs 把成員商品分開（一成員一 tab），每個 tab 面板（.tab-panel）放該成員的規格表。只有一層 tab（成員），規格不用 tab；數量跨 tab 保留。商品細節頁補貨紀錄重用 .data-list。由 partials/restock-modal.js 掛載。

Three number columns per row: Current and After are read-only (.restock-table__ro, muted, not typeable); only Restock takes input, and After recomputes live as current + restock.

每列三欄數字：當前與補後唯讀（.restock-table__ro，靜音底、不可打字），只有補貨可填，補後隨補貨即時算成「當前＋補貨」。

每列依選項一以 .restock-table__group 分組（Small／Medium）。組合以成員 tab 分開每個商品、各自一張表；單一選項商品則是一張只有一列、無分組標題的表。

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Keep the 2026-07-22 order: method (radio-cards) → product-name label → .restock-table → supplier / notes / ETA below; pin the footer to the dialog bottom, scroll only the body.
  • 照 2026-07-22 順序：方式（radio-cards）→ 商品名稱標題 → .restock-table → 供應商／備註／到貨在下方；footer 釘框底、只捲 body。
  • Keep Current and After read-only (.restock-table__ro); only Restock is typeable — stock rises only through a logged restock.
  • 當前與補後維持唯讀（.restock-table__ro），只有補貨可填——庫存只透過有紀錄的補貨上升。
  • Group a multi-variant product or bundle member with .restock-table__group; bundle members = .tabs (one tab per member product, D106).
  • 多選項商品或組合成員以 .restock-table__group 分組；組合成員＝.tabs（一成員一 tab，D106）。
Don't別做
  • Don't fork the dialog / form / segmented / tabs / data-list styles — only the .restock-table rows are restock-specific.
  • 別 fork dialog／表單／segmented／tabs／data-list 樣式 — 只有 .restock-table 列是 restock 專屬。
  • Don't put method / supplier / ETA on each row, and don't bring back the under-method hint row or the yellow stickynote — the 2026-07-22 layout removed them.
  • 別把方式／供應商／到貨放進每列，也別找回方式下的提示行或黃色 stickynote——2026-07-22 版型已移除。
  • Don't tab variants or nest tabs — only member products get tabs; variants stay a table (avoids two-level tabs).
  • 別把規格做成 tab、別巢狀 tab — 只有成員商品用 tab，規格維持表格（避免兩層 tab）。

4.66 Composer

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

Drop-or-type input card with a bottom action bar: left tool icons, right credit meter and a circular send button that flips to orange when there's content. Use when a creator submits a prompt or uploads an asset and you need a single card combining input, tool affordances, credit meter, and submit. Avoid for plain single-line fields.

可拖放或輸入的輸入卡，底部有動作列：左側工具圖示、右側 credit 計量與一個圓形送出按鈕，有內容時翻成橘色。當創作者要送出 prompt 或上傳素材，而你需要一張卡片同時整合輸入、工具提示、credit 計量與送出時使用。純單行欄位別用。

4.68 Alert

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

Inline notice with a status-tinted icon, title, description, optional CTA, and (card density) a chevron close button. Use .alert--card in the dashboard alerts panel; .alert--row for inline page warnings (low-stock, region). Avoid for a single editorial hint — use the Info banner.

行內通知，含一個帶狀態色調的圖示、標題、說明、可選的 CTA，以及（card 版型時）一個 chevron 關閉按鈕。dashboard 警示面板用 .alert--card；頁面行內警告（低庫存、地區）用 .alert--row。單則編輯性提示別用 — 改用 Info banner。

Notification bar (.alert--bar — single-line bar: rounded corners + soft shadow, no divider; .alert__title + inline .alert__meta, optional .alert__cta, .alert__dismiss ✕. Add .alert--page-top for sticky full-bleed edge-to-edge page-top placement inside the app shell. Two usages: Events' Event Day scenario banner (injected by js/scenario.js) uses the base as-is; E-Shop's low-stock bar (F2) narrows and centers it to the content column via an instance override, shadow swapped for .edge-shadow — a documented page-level exception)

通知條 (.alert--bar — 單行通知條：圓角＋陰影、無線段；.alert__title＋同行 .alert__meta、選配 .alert__cta、.alert__dismiss ✕。加 .alert--page-top 變貼頂滿版邊到邊常駐通知條。兩個使用情境：Events 的 Event Day 情境橫幅（js/scenario.js 注入）用基底原樣；E-Shop 低庫存提醒（F2）以 instance 覆寫收窄置中對齊內容欄、陰影改走 .edge-shadow，屬記錄在案的頁面特例)

⚠
3 products below low-stock threshold

Do該做
  • Match the status modifier to severity.
  • 讓狀態修飾子對應嚴重程度。
  • Use a filled Tabler glyph in .alert__icon.

Don't別做
  • Add a close button to .alert--row.
  • 別給 .alert--row 加關閉按鈕。

4.69 Notification matrix

🟠 organism

Event-type (rows) × channel (columns) grid of per-cell toggles for Settings → Notifications (spec 5.1.9 F3). Each event switches on/off independently per Email / Push / In-app. Compliance channels (payout / KYC / compliance · Email) are locked on with a lock glyph and the reason in the title.

設定 → 通知（規格 5.1.9 F3）用的「事件型別(列) × 管道(欄)」逐格開關矩陣。每個事件在 Email／Push／站內各自獨立開關。合規通道（提款／KYC／合規 的 Email）鎖定為開啟，顯示鎖頭、原因寫在 title。

Event
Email
Push
In-app
Sales & orders
Order, fulfilment, payout result.
Compliance alert
Caps, holds, jurisdiction limits affecting payouts.
For developers — classes · code給工程師 — class · 程式碼

.notif-matrix · __corner / __chead / __label(__label-title/__label-hint) / __cell(.--locked) / __lock。每格放一顆 .switch；鎖定格用 .switch--on.switch--locked + lock icon，原因寫 title。grid =「label 欄 + 3 管道欄」。

4.70 Status axes

🟡 molecule

Two independent order status tracks shown together (spec 5.1.5.3.1 §2.2 / PCR-001): fulfilment (履約: To ship / Shipped / Delivered) and payment·settlement (收入結算: Paid / Refunded / Disputed). They are never merged into one badge. .status-axes = badges side by side (list rows, fulfilment first); .status-axes--labeled stacks each under an uppercase label (order detail header). Badges come from badge.css — Paid uses badge--success (green, Q11 2026-07-13; was badge--neutral).

訂單兩條獨立狀態軸並列（規格 5.1.5.3.1 §2.2 / PCR-001）：履約（To ship／Shipped／Delivered）與收入結算（Paid／Refunded／Disputed），不併成單一 badge。.status-axes＝badge 並排（清單列，履約在前）；.status-axes--labeled 每軸在大寫標籤下堆疊（訂單詳情頁首）。badge 取自 badge.css——Paid 用 badge--success（綠色，Q11 2026-07-13；原為 badge--neutral）。

FulfilmentTo ship
Payment · settlementPaid
ShippedDisputed
For developers — classes · code給工程師 — class · 程式碼

.status-axes (inline badges, list rows) · .status-axes--labeled > .status-axis > .status-axis__label + .badge (detail header). Fulfilment and payment·settlement are separate axes (§7.2) — never combined. Used in orders.html rows + order-detail.html §2.2.

4.71 Chart

🟠 organism

Purpose

用途

SVG-based visualization family with five sub-patterns (line chart, bar chart, stacked bar, source-list legend, rank bars) plus a .chart-card composition shell and a JS-driven tooltip/cursor layer. Use .linechart for trends, .barchart for discrete values, .stacked-bar + .source-list for a proportion breakdown, .rank-bars for ranked rows, and .chart-card to wrap with head + footer; avoid for exact tabular figures — use .ztor-table.

以 SVG 為基礎的視覺化家族，含五種 sub-pattern（line chart、bar chart、stacked bar、source-list legend、rank bars），外加一個 .chart-card 組合外殼與 JS 驅動的 tooltip／cursor 層。趨勢用 .linechart，離散值用 .barchart，比例拆解用 .stacked-bar + .source-list，排名列用 .rank-bars，要包 head + footer 用 .chart-card；要精確的表格數字別用 — 改用 .ztor-table。

4.72 Earnings waterfall

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

A statement-style vertical ledger (spec §5.1.8 F12) that walks gross revenue down to distributable profit and its Creator / NFT split. Reads like a P&L — milestones (income / subtotal / pool / distribution) carry a running-balance bar; deductions are plain indented name … −amount rows with no bar, so it doesn't become a wall of bars. Figures follow §7.3 (only settled income counts). Used on the Earnings · Breakdown tab and reused for the F11 per-project ladder and the F7 transaction mini-ladder.

報表式垂直帳本（spec §5.1.8 F12），把總收入一路走到可分配淨利與 Creator／NFT 分配。讀起來像損益表——里程碑（income／subtotal／pool／distribution）帶 running-balance 條；扣項是純文字縮排 名稱 … −金額 列、不帶條，避免變成一面 bar 牆。數字口徑依 §7.3（僅計已結算收入）。用於 Earnings · Breakdown 分頁，並重用於 F11 單一專案階梯與 F7 交易小階梯。

Relationships

元件關係

Built from由哪些元件組成 ↓
self-containedlabel + meta + proportional bar; no atom children標籤＋說明＋比例條；無 atom 子元件

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Set each __fill width to the running balance as a % of gross — the descending staircase is the point.
  • 把每條 __fill 寬度設為「該階後的 running balance ÷ 總收入」%——下降的階梯就是重點。
  • Mark milestones with --subtotal / --pool and allocations with --distribution.
  • 里程碑用 --subtotal／--pool，分配列用 --distribution 標示。
Don't別做
  • Don't render $0 rows to fake a full waterfall — use .waterfall__empty when there is no settled income.
  • 別用 $0 列假裝完整瀑布——沒有已結算收入時改用 .waterfall__empty。
  • Don't put unsettled / disputed amounts into distributable profit (§7.3).
  • 別把未結算／爭議中金額算進可分配淨利（§7.3）。
For developers — classes · tokens · code給工程師 — class · token · 程式碼

Class API (CSS classes — Props/API N/A, static prototype)

Class API（樣式類別） （CSS classes — 無 Props/API，靜態原型）

Class / modifierClass／修飾子Effect效果
.waterfall / .waterfall__row / __head / __name / __meta / __amtLedger column; each row = label + meta + right amount + full-width bar帳本欄；每列＝標籤＋說明＋右側金額＋滿寬條
.waterfall__bar / .waterfall__fillMuted track + fill; set width inline to the running balance %淺底 track＋fill；width 行內設為 running balance %
--income / --deduct / --subtotal / --pool / --distributionRow types: source / a cut (grey bar, − amount) / milestone (rule + bold) / distributable profit (orange fill) / indented allocation列型：來源／扣項（灰條、−金額）／里程碑（分隔線＋粗體）／可分配淨利（橘色 fill）／縮排分配
--pool.waterfall__row--negativeDistributable-profit-negative warning: error-tinted bar + amount (distribution paused, §7.3)可分配淨利為負示警：error 色條＋金額（分配暫停，§7.3）
.waterfall__emptyEmpty state — no settled income this period (don't fake $0)空狀態——本期間無已結算收入（不假裝 $0）

4.77 Leave dialog

🟠 organism

Confirm-before-leaving dialog for every create / edit flow (spec §5.2.4). Injected and driven by partials/wizard-chrome.js, shared by all 6 create pages. Two states, one shell: when the page has unsaved edits it asks about saving (Save and leave / Leave without saving); when nothing was edited it just confirms leaving (Leave) — no save question. Capped card, dimmed scrim, title + body + stacked actions + corner close.

建立／編輯流程的「返回離開確認」彈窗（規格 §5.2.4）。由 partials/wizard-chrome.js 注入並控制，6 個建立頁共用。兩個型態、同一外殼：頁面有未存編輯時問儲存（儲存並離開／不儲存就離開）；沒編輯過則只確認離開（離開）、不問儲存。有上限的卡、變暗 scrim、標題＋內文＋堆疊操作＋右上關閉。

要先儲存再離開嗎？

這一頁有你做的編輯。

要離開這一頁嗎？

你隨時可以再回來。

4.79 Album tracks

🟠 organism

Multi-track manager for digital products whose sub-category is Album (spec 5.1.5.2 §4.2 F11.1). Empty state shows a "No files uploaded yet" placeholder. Upload multiple audio (mp3) / video (mp4) files; each becomes a track row with a cover, editable name, file meta (name · size · time), drag-to-reorder handle, and a ⋮ menu (Edit name · Change image · Upload lyrics · Delete). Hovering the cover reveals play/pause + edit (change image). Uploading rows show "…is uploading…" with an indeterminate bar and no drag handle. Lyrics are audio-only — after Upload lyrics a "View Lyrics" button appears; video tracks have no lyrics. Reuses the .dropdown menu component. Click to try below.

數位商品次分類為音樂專輯（Album）時的多曲目管理器（spec 5.1.5.2 §4.2 F11.1）。空狀態顯示「尚未上傳任何檔案」佔位訊息。上傳多個音訊（mp3）／影片（mp4）檔，每檔一列曲目：封面、可改曲名、檔案 meta（檔名·大小·時間）、拖曳把手、⋯ 選單（改名·換封面·上傳歌詞·刪除）。hover 封面浮現 播放/暫停＋編輯（換封面）。上傳中列顯示「上傳中…」＋不定進度條、無拖曳把手。歌詞為音訊限定——上傳歌詞後出現「查看歌詞」；影片曲目無歌詞。重用 .dropdown 選單元件。可在下方點擊試用。

Note: presentation-layer demo — upload / lyrics / cover are faked (files shown via object URL, no real upload or storage). Track-field product details (min 1 track, cover required, lyrics format, size limits, preview) are TBC upstream (recorded in ASSUMPTIONS).

注意：呈現層 demo——上傳／歌詞／封面皆為假動作（檔案以 object URL 顯示，無真實上傳或儲存）。曲目欄位的產品細節（至少一曲、封面必填、歌詞格式、大小上限、試聽）待上游確認（已記 ASSUMPTIONS）。

4.83 Mobile scanner

🟠 organism

Standalone phone scanner (spec 5.1.5.14 F1 · D111/D121) — a separate URL with no Studio nav. Staff enter the session password, then scan buyer QR codes to redeem. Camera viewport uses the --surface-inverse role token (not a raw dark hex). Screens: password gate → scan → result → confirm. After unlock, a Scan/Items/Roster sub-nav also exposes F2 verifiable items (canonical definition) and F3 a read-only check-in roster for manual lookup when a QR can't be scanned — neither links out to other Studio pages, matching the scanner's permission boundary.

獨立手機 scanner（規格 5.1.5.14 F1 · D111/D121）——獨立 URL、無主工作台導航。工作人員輸入場次密碼後掃買家 QR 核銷。相機視窗用 --surface-inverse role token（非裸色深色）。畫面：密碼→掃描→結果→確認。解鎖後多一列 Scan／Items／Roster 分頁，分別是 F2 可核銷項目（正式定義）與 F3 唯讀取貨/入場名單（QR 無法掃描時人工查詢核對）——皆不連出其他工作台頁面，對齊 scanner 的權限邊界。

4.84 Radio list

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

Lightweight vertical 1-of-N picker: a radio dot + title (optional one-line sub) per row; a filled orange dot marks the selection. Lighter than Selection card (no card frame/shadow) and, unlike Segmented, it is a data choice rather than a view switch. Two variants: base keeps every option visible; --collapsible (2026-07-21, Figma 856-22782) shows only the current selection plus a chevron and reveals the full list on click — use it when the picker sits in a narrow column and vertical space is scarce, e.g. Listing settings (Don't list / List now / Schedule) under the store-preview card. In the collapsible variant the selected option appears twice while open (once in the trigger, once in the list) — that is the intended Figma behaviour. Independent component (own classes + JS), not built on Segmented.

輕量垂直單選：每列一個 radio 圓點＋標題（可帶一句描述），圓點填橘＝選中。比 Selection card 輕（無卡框陰影）；與 Segmented 的分工是它做資料選擇、不是視角切換。兩個變體：base 選項恆展開；--collapsible（2026-07-21，Figma 856-22782）收起時只顯示目前選項＋chevron，點一下才展開完整清單，用於窄欄、垂直空間吃緊的情境——例如商店預覽卡下的上架設定（不上架／立刻上架／定時上架）。收合式展開時已選項會出現兩次（觸發列一次、清單一次），這是 Figma 原設計、刻意保留。獨立元件（自有 class＋JS），非建在 Segmented 上。

Rendered preview

視覺展示

Base — every option visibleBase — 選項恆展開

--collapsible — click the trigger to open--collapsible — 點觸發列展開

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Use for mutually-exclusive data choices; pick --collapsible when vertical space is scarce.
  • 用於互斥的資料選擇；垂直空間吃緊時選 --collapsible。
  • Sit it on a white / --card surface (hover uses --accent).
  • 放在白／--card 底上（hover 用 --accent）。
Don't別做
  • Use it to switch the view of one dataset — that's Segmented.
  • 別用在切換同一資料的視角（那是 Segmented）。
  • Mix both variants for the same role on different pages — Listing settings is collapsible everywhere.
  • 別讓同一角色在不同頁用不同變體——上架設定全站一律收合式。

Specification

規格

Sourceradio-list.css · partials/radio-list.js (collapsible behaviour)
AnatomyBase: .radio-list > .radio-list__item (--active) > .radio-list__dot + .radio-list__text (__title + optional __sub).
Collapsible: .radio-list.radio-list--collapsible[data-open] > .radio-list__trigger (dot + text + .radio-list__chevron) + .radio-list__options[hidden] > .radio-list__item.
Variants(base) every option visible · --collapsible trigger + disclosure list, 1px --border frame at --radius-xl, open trigger fills --input-surface, chevron rotates 180°.
Statesdefault · hover (--accent) · focus-visible (--ring) · selected (--active, orange filled dot) · open / closed ([data-open], collapsible only).
Behavior / usageVertical flex; transparent rows, hover --accent; selected = orange filled dot (--primary), no bg/border change. Rows with no .radio-list__sub vertically center dot + title. partials/radio-list.js auto-mounts every .radio-list--collapsible: toggles open state, mirrors the selected row's text + data-i18n keys into the trigger, closes on outside click / Esc, and dispatches radio-list:change (detail.item) so pages only own their own field-reveal logic.
Token usage--foreground, --accent, --muted-foreground, --primary, --border, --input-surface, --ring, --radius-md, --radius-xl, --sp-2/8/10, --fs-14/12, --duration, --easing.

4.85 Date input placeholder

🔵 atom

Purpose

用途

Native <input type="date|datetime-local|time"> ignores placeholder and paints its own 年/月/日 --:-- mask in ordinary body colour, so an untouched field reads as already filled. This decorator replaces the empty state with the same placeholder language every other field uses: calendar icon + muted "Pick a date". Filled state is untouched — the date renders in normal body colour at the field's original padding, so no layout shifts. Applied automatically site-wide by partials/date-input.js; pages keep plain <input class="input" type="date"> markup.

原生 <input type="date|datetime-local|time"> 不吃 placeholder，空值時瀏覽器自己畫「年/月/日 --:--」且用一般內文色，看起來像已經填了值。本裝飾層把空值狀態換成站上其他欄位一致的 placeholder 語言：日曆 icon ＋ 淡灰「選擇日期」。已填狀態完全不動——日期用正常內文色、內距回到欄位原值，不造成任何位移。由 partials/date-input.js 全站自動套用，頁面 markup 維持乾淨的 <input class="input" type="date">。

Rendered preview

視覺展示

Empty — icon + placeholder空值 — icon ＋ placeholder

Filled — plain body colour, original padding已填 — 正常內文色、原始內距

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Leave page markup as a bare .input — the decorator wraps it at runtime.
  • 頁面 markup 就寫乾淨的 .input，包裝交給執行期的裝飾層。
  • Call ZtorDateInput.mount(scope) only if you bypass the DOM observer.
  • 只有繞過 DOM observer 時才需要自己呼叫 ZtorDateInput.mount(scope)。
Don't別做
  • Hand-write .date-input wrappers in pages — duplicated markup drifts.
  • 別在頁面手寫 .date-input 外層，重複 markup 會分岔。
  • Keep the icon visible when filled — it eats 28px and clips narrow fields.
  • 別讓 icon 在已填狀態留著——它吃掉 28px，窄欄會被切字。

Specification

規格

Sourcedate-input.css · partials/date-input.js
Anatomy.date-input[data-empty] > .date-input__icon + .input + .date-input__ph. The wrapper, icon and placeholder are injected at runtime; pages only author the .input.
States[data-empty="true"] calendar icon at --sp-12 + "Pick a date" at --sp-40 in --muted-foreground, native ::-webkit-datetime-edit hidden, input padded to --sp-40 · [data-empty="false"] icon and placeholder hidden, padding back to the base --sp-12, date in --foreground.
Behavior / usageCovers date, datetime-local and time — all three share the "Pick a date" copy (field.pick-date) per the 2026-07-21 ruling. The native calendar button is flattened into a transparent full-field overlay, so clicking anywhere opens the picker via showPicker(). A MutationObserver catches runtime-injected fields (restock, pickup session, manual entry, product post modals) so partials need no wiring of their own.
Token usage--muted-foreground, --foreground, --font-body, --fs-14, --sp-12, --sp-40.
Classes.date-input · .date-input__icon · .date-input__ph
DependenciesDecorates Input; composes Icon (calendar).
Evidence / usage~40 date fields across 17 pages: create-product · create-bundle · create-auction · create-event · create-campaign · create-project · product-detail · bundle-detail · settings · fans-crm · admin-platform-fees · ip-bank-reporting · pickup · pickup-detail · e-shop · earnings, plus the restock / pickup-session / manual-entry / product-post modals.
NoteThis page has no data-i18n runtime, so the demo placeholder stays English in both language modes; product pages resolve field.pick-date normally.

4.87 Stock readout

🔵 atom

Purpose

用途

A read-only quantity shown as a big number rather than an input, for values that can only change through a specific action. Product detail uses it for stock: units are added by Restock (every restock is logged), so rendering it as an .input would imply you can type over it. The optional denominator (a Limited edition cap) and the unit both live in __unit, keeping the number itself the single focal point.

唯讀的數量，用大數字而非輸入框呈現——適用於「只能透過某個特定動作改變」的值。商品明細的庫存用它：庫存只能靠補貨增加（每筆留紀錄），做成 .input 會讓人以為可以打字覆蓋。可選的分母（限量版本的上限）與單位都收在 __unit 裡，讓數值本身維持單一焦點。

Rendered preview

視覺展示

3 units Low Stock
To add units, use Restock on the right — every restock is logged.
18 / 50 units
Limited edition — the cap goes in the unit slot, no badge needed.

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Pair it with a hint naming the action that changes the number.
  • 配一句 hint 說明「要改這個數字得做什麼」。
  • Put the cap and unit together in __unit.
  • 分母與單位一起放進 __unit。
Don't別做
  • Don't use KPI here — that's a bordered tile for dashboards; this is a line inside a form card.
  • 別拿 KPI 來用——那是儀表列用的有框方塊，這個是表單卡內的一行讀數。
  • Don't render an editable .input for a value the user can't actually type into.
  • 使用者其實不能打字的值，別做成可編輯的 .input。

Specification

規格

Sourcestock-readout.css
Anatomy.stock-readout > .stock-readout__num + .stock-readout__unit + optional Badge. Baseline-aligned flex row; no container styling of its own (it sits inside a .field).
Behavior / usageRead-only. The consumer decides whether to show a status badge (low stock / sold out) and swaps the denominator in when the edition is Limited. Product detail hides the / 50 span unless [data-when-edition="limited"].
Token usage--font-display, --fs-28, --fw-medium, --foreground（數值）; --fs-13, --muted-foreground（單位）; --sp-8, --sp-6. Letter-spacing −0.6px 為顯示字體的視覺補償，非 token。
Classes.stock-readout · .stock-readout__num · .stock-readout__unit
DependenciesComposes Badge (optional). Distinct from KPI — see Do & Don't.
Evidence / usageproduct-detail (single-option stock).

4.88 Restock log

🟡 molecule

Purpose

用途

A restock history table: one row per restock, each field in its own aligned column. Restock records exist to be compared — how many more units than last time, how long since the previous restock — and columns are what make that scannable. It replaces the earlier Data list treatment that packed quantity, date and supplier into a title line plus a meta line, which could only be read one entry at a time. The --with-option modifier opens the option-combination column for multi-option products; without it that column disappears entirely, header included.

補貨紀錄表：每一筆補貨佔一列，每個欄位各自成欄地對齊。補貨紀錄是拿來比對的——這批比上批多幾件、上次補貨隔了多久——欄位對齊才掃得動。它取代原本用 Data list 把數量、日期、供應商擠成一行標題＋一行 meta 的寫法，那種寫法只能一筆一筆讀。多選項商品掛 --with-option 開出「選項組合」欄；不掛時該欄連同表頭整欄不顯示。

Relationships

元件關係

Built from由哪些元件組成 ↓
atomBadge
Used by被哪些元件使用 ↑
Sits directly in a Form section card on the consumer page直接放在 consumer 頁的 Form section 卡裡

Rendered preview (both states — four columns by default, five with --with-option)

視覺展示 (兩種狀態——預設四欄，掛 --with-option 為五欄)

Single-option product — no option column單選項商品——沒有選項組合欄

Option選項組合 Quantity補貨數量 Date日期 Supplier供應商 Status狀態
— +40 2026/06/18 Riso House Completed已入庫
— +25 2026/05/02 Riso House Completed已入庫

Multi-option product — .restock-log--with-option多選項商品——.restock-log--with-option

Option選項組合 Quantity補貨數量 Date日期 Supplier供應商 Status狀態
Black / M +120 2026/07/18 Tainan Studio Completed已入庫
Black / S +8 2026/07/02 Tainan Studio Scheduled已排程

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Put quantities in .restock-log__qty so tabular numerals line the digits up across rows.
  • 補貨數量放進 .restock-log__qty，等寬數字才會讓上下列的位數對齊。
  • Let .restock-log-wrap scroll horizontally on narrow viewports — columns stay aligned instead of reflowing.
  • 窄視窗讓 .restock-log-wrap 水平捲動——欄位維持對齊，不重排。
Don't別做
  • Don't hide the option cell row by row — the header and every row share one grid-template-columns, so removing a cell in only one place misaligns the table. Toggle --with-option on the container instead.
  • 別逐列隱藏選項儲存格——表頭與每一列共用同一組 grid-template-columns，只在其中一處拿掉會讓欄位錯位。改為在容器上切換 --with-option。
  • Don't put editable controls in a row — this is read-only history. For an editable priced spec table use the Variant builder.
  • 別把可編輯控件放進列裡——本元件是唯讀歷史。要可編輯的逐規格價格表請用 Variant builder。

Anatomy.restock-log-wrap > .restock-log(--with-option) > .restock-log__head + .restock-log__row. Cells: .restock-log__opt (option combination — the header cell carries the same class) · .restock-log__qty (quantity, tabular numerals) · .restock-log__muted (date / supplier) · Badge (status).
Statesdefault — four columns, .restock-log__opt is display:none · .restock-log--with-option — five columns, the option cell returns to display:block in both header and rows · .restock-log__row:last-child — bottom hairline zeroed so it doesn't double with the wrapper border.

Column widths use the same grid technique as Variant builder's spec table but deliberately share nothing with it — that one is editable configuration, this one is read-only history.

4.89 Stock tip

🟢 atom

Purpose

用途

Hover or focus any product row's "Status" or "Stock" cell in the E-Shop product list → a small floating info card. For multi-option or bundle rows, it lists every option combination's own stock count (bundle members flattened down to their own option combinations too). Promoted 2026-07-23 from user feedback — wanting the per-option breakdown visible without opening the Restock popup. Scope was widened the same day: asked why single-variant rows (zine, acetate, pin) didn't get it too — for those rows the card restates current stock (with its real health colour). It briefly also showed a computed low-stock threshold line, added then removed the same day on user instruction — the threshold logic (lowThr(), 10% of cap) still lives in the shared data layer for the Restock popup, it just isn't surfaced in this card anymore.

hover 或 focus 電子商店商品清單裡任何一列的「狀態」或「庫存」欄 → 浮出一張小卡。多選項或組合商品列會列出每個選項組合各自的庫存（組合商品連成員都攤到成員自己的選項組合）。2026-07-23 依使用者反饋 promote——想在不開補貨彈窗的情況下就看到逐選項的庫存。同一天擴大範圍：使用者追問「為什麼單一選項商品（zine、acetate、pin）沒有」——這些列改顯示「目前庫存」一行（照實際健康度上色）。中間曾短暫多顯示一行低庫存門檻，同一天使用者又指示拿掉——門檻換算邏輯（lowThr()，cap 的 10%）仍留在共用資料層給補貨彈窗用，只是這張浮卡不再顯示。

Relationships

元件關係

Built from由哪些元件組成 ↓
No sub-components — plain floating card沒有子元件——單純的浮出卡
Used by被哪些元件使用 ↑
Sits directly on Product list's status/stock cells直接掛在 Product list 的狀態／庫存儲存格上

Why JS positions it, not pure CSS :hover

為什麼定位靠 JS、不是純 CSS :hover

The list scrolls under a sticky filter bar (E-Shop's .list-toolbar / .list-status-row). A row near the top of the viewport would have its popup covered by the sticky bar if it always opened upward; a row near the bottom would push the popup off-screen if it always opened downward. JS measures the trigger's getBoundingClientRect() on mouseenter/focusin, flips direction based on whether the row sits in the top or bottom half of the viewport, and sets position: fixed coordinates directly — plain CSS can't see viewport position to make that call.

清單捲動在一個有 sticky 篩選列的容器裡（電子商店的 .list-toolbar／.list-status-row）。固定往上開，viewport 上緣的列會被 sticky 列蓋到；固定往下開，viewport 下緣的列會把浮卡推出可視範圍。JS 在 mouseenter／focusin 量測觸發格的 getBoundingClientRect()，依列在 viewport 上半部或下半部翻轉開啟方向，直接設定 position: fixed 座標——純 CSS 看不到 viewport 位置，做不了這個判斷。

Rendered preview (static — hover state forced open for the demo; live pages position via JS on hover/focus)

視覺展示 (靜態展示——demo 直接強制顯示開啟狀態；實際頁面靠 JS 在 hover/focus 時定位)

1-axis multi-option (e.g. tee sizes)單軸多選項（如 tee 尺寸）

Current stock目前庫存3

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Generate the popup content from the same variant data the Restock popup reads — never hand-type a second copy of the numbers.
  • 浮卡內容從補貨彈窗讀的同一份選項資料產生——別另外手key第二份數字。
  • Keep both cells' content identical for now (status cell and stock cell both show the full option breakdown).
  • 目前兩個欄位的內容維持一樣（狀態欄、庫存欄都顯示完整的選項明細）。
  • When the row's badge is "Low Stock" (e-shop.row.low), filter the list down to just the options that need restocking — omit the healthy ones entirely rather than just de-emphasizing them.
  • 列徽章是「急需補貨」（e-shop.row.low）時，清單只留需要補貨的選項——健康的選項直接不列，不是弱化顯示就好。
Don't別做
  • Don't leave a native title attribute on a cell that also carries .stock-tip — they compete on the same hover, stacking a browser-native tooltip on top of the custom popup (found on the acetate row's stock cell, removed 2026-07-23).
  • 別在掛了 .stock-tip 的儲存格上留原生 title 屬性——兩套 hover 提示會互搶，瀏覽器原生 tooltip 疊在自訂浮卡上面（acetate 列的庫存欄踩過，2026-07-23 移除）。
  • Don't put data-i18n directly on .stock-tip — i18n.js's innerHTML swap would wipe the .stock-tip__pop child. Wrap the translatable text in its own <span data-i18n> sibling instead.
  • 別把 data-i18n直接掛在 .stock-tip 上——i18n.js 的 innerHTML 覆寫會把子節點 .stock-tip__pop 一起清掉。可翻譯文字改包一層 <span data-i18n>手足。

Specification

規格

Sourcestock-tip.css
Anatomy.stock-tip (trigger cell, position: relative) > .stock-tip__pop (position: fixed card, role="tooltip") > .stock-tip__row (.stock-tip__name + .stock-tip__qty, --low/--out modifiers colour the quantity).
Statesdefault (closed) — opacity:0; visibility:hidden · .stock-tip.is-open (JS-added on mouseenter/focusin, removed on mouseleave/focusout) — popup fades in, position set inline by JS.
Behavior / usageContent is pre-populated once per row on page load into both the status cell's and the stock cell's .stock-tip__pop — only the position is recomputed on every hover. Rows with option data (from the same PRODUCT_MATRIX/PRODUCT_VARIANTS/BUNDLE_MEMBERS the Restock popup reads) get the per-option breakdown; if the row's status cell contains [data-i18n="e-shop.row.low"] ("Low Stock"), that list is filtered to just the low/out entries before rendering (2026-07-23). Rows without option data (single-variant) get one line instead (2026-07-23, scope widened): current stock, colour reflecting row[data-status] — the option-health filter above doesn't apply to it. A low-stock threshold line was briefly shown here too; removed same day on user instruction (the threshold math still lives in the shared data layer for the Restock popup).
Token usage--card (bg) · --shadow-float (E3, same rung as dropdown/readiness pops) · --radius-md · --foreground / --foreground-muted (label) · --status-warning / --status-error (quantity colour) · --fs-12 / --fw-medium / --lh-normal.
Classes.stock-tip · .stock-tip__pop · .stock-tip__row · .stock-tip__name · .stock-tip__qty(--low/--out)
DependenciesNone — plain CSS, no composed component.
Evidence / usagee-shop.html — every row of the Products tab (zine/tee/hoodie/acetate/pin) and both rows of the Bundles tab.

4.86 Nest

🔵 atom

Purpose

用途

A full-bleed block seated at the bottom of a card: its left, right and bottom edges meet the card's outer edge, and an upward-cast shadow lifts it off the card face. Use it when flipping a mode grows a whole set of controls below — e.g. switching Variations to "Multiple" in create-product. Aligned to Figma node 856:27798.

嵌在卡片底部的滿版子層：左右與下緣切齊卡片外緣，靠一道向上打的陰影跟卡面分開。用在「切換某個模式後，下方長出一整組設定」的情境——例如建立商品的商品選項切到「多選項」。對齊 Figma node 856:27798。

Rendered preview (toggle the theme — light separates by shadow alone, dark adds a translucent film)

視覺展示 （切換日／夜看差別——亮色只靠陰影分層，深色多疊一層半透明薄膜）

Variations

The nest below is flush with the card's own edges.

Two fills only — layer 3 and beyond use borders

只有兩層填色——第三層以後改用邊框

L1 card --card (absolute) → L2 nest --nest-surface (translucent film). Stacking a third fill makes every layer muddier and washes the canvas's colour temperature out, so depth beyond L2 is carried by a 1px border instead. The rule is not written into nest.css — a nest doesn't know what will be placed inside it, and a blanket .nest > * would hit the wrong things. Consumers apply it themselves; first case is Variant builder's .option-set__row / .variant-option, which dropped their --input-surface fill for transparent + 1px --border. L3 borders have no dedicated token — reuse --border.

L1 卡片 --card（絕對色）→ L2 nest --nest-surface（半透明薄膜）。再往上疊第三層填色會讓每一層都愈來愈糊、也把畫布的色溫洗掉，所以 L2 以後的層級改用 1px 邊框表達。這條規則不寫在 nest.css 裡——nest 不知道自己裡面會放什麼，硬寫 .nest > * 會誤傷；由消費端自己套。首個落地案例是 Variant builder 的 .option-set__row／.variant-option，它們把 --input-surface 填色換成 transparent ＋ 1px --border。L3 邊框沒有專屬 token，就用 --border。

Why a cool-grey film, not plain white: a white overlay neutralises the midnight canvas's cool cast (B−R drops from +2 to +0.8). The tint rgb(222,223,233) pushes it to +3.0 instead, staying the same temperature as the canvas. Same value Figma arrived at independently (856:27796).

為什麼用冷調薄膜、不用純白：純白疊上去會把 midnight 畫布的冷色調洗掉（B−R 由 +2 掉到 +0.8）。改用 rgb(222,223,233) 這個 tint 反而把冷調推到 +3.0，與畫布同溫。Figma 獨立算出的也是同一個值（856:27796）。

Do & Don't

該做與別做

Do該做
  • Put it last inside the card — it is anchored to the bottom edge.
  • 放在卡片的最後一個子元素——它是貼著底緣長的。
  • Use .card--muted instead for a static sub-block that keeps the card's inner padding.
  • 只是「卡片裡的一段」而且要保留卡片內距時，改用 .card--muted。
Don't別做
  • Don't put a dropdown or popover in a card that holds a nest — the card is clipped.
  • 含 nest 的卡片裡別放 dropdown／popover——那張卡被裁切，浮層會被切掉。
  • Don't stack a third fill inside a nest; use a border.
  • 別在 nest 裡再疊第三層填色，用邊框。

Specification

規格

Sourcenest.css
AnatomySingle block. Negative margins (calc(var(--sp-16) * -1)) cancel the parent card's --sp-16 padding on left / right / bottom; --sp-16 top margin keeps the gap from the preceding control.
Behavior / usageborder-radius matches the parent card's --radius-xl exactly, because the three edges are coincident. The parent is clipped via .form-section--outlined:has(> .nest) { overflow: hidden; } — required, because --shadow-nest-up has only a vertical offset and its 8px blur would otherwise spill sideways past the card's rounded corners onto the page. .nest[hidden] forces display:none so a consumer's own display:flex can't leak through.
Token usage--nest-surface（dark rgba(222,223,233,.04) / light transparent）, --shadow-nest-up（dark 0 -8px 8px rgba(0,0,0,.08) / light 0 -6px 8px rgba(0,0,0,.05)）, --radius-xl, --sp-16.
Classes.nest
DependenciesRequires a Form section .form-section--outlined parent. Distinct from Card .card--muted — see Do & Don't.
Evidence / usagecreate-product — Variations builder (#cp-var-builder), shown in Multiple-variations mode.
05.1 · Pattern ▸ Cards

How components assemble.元件如何組合

Best-practice assembly recipes — how components combine to meet a creator's goal. Ten cards across four categories (page-level and mid-level); each has trigger / must / should / must-not / edge-cases. Component sections demo the unit only — assembly rules live here.

最佳實務的組合配方 — 元件如何組合起來達成創作者的目標。四個類別共十張卡（頁面級＋中間層），每張都列出 trigger / must / should / must-not / edge-cases。元件段只展示單元本身——組合規則一律寫在這裡（判準見 §4.0）。

LayoutLayoutDetail + persistent railDetail + persistent railAn entity page where editing is split across tabs but a few read-only facts must never leave view (product detail: stock, delivery, linked project) → wrap the page in .page.page--narrow (1056px — the default 1280px plus a 300px rail leaves the main column too wide), then the Detail rail shell: editable Tabs in .detail-main, sticky .detail-rail on the right holding read-only Form section cards built from KV list / Stock bar / KPI. The rail answers "what do I need to know before I change something", so it holds constraints and consequences (stock on hand, delivery method, what this item is attached to), never the fields being edited and never a primary action. Cap it at 3–4 cards — a rail that scrolls has stopped being persistent. Below 1100px it falls in under the main column, so nothing in it may be the only route to a task.編輯分散在多個分頁、但有幾項唯讀事實必須永遠看得到的實體頁（商品細節：庫存、交付、關聯專案）→ 頁面外層用 .page.page--narrow（1056px——預設 1280px 再配 300px 右欄，主欄會太寬），內層用 Detail rail 殼：可編輯的 Tabs 放 .detail-main，右邊 sticky 的 .detail-rail 放唯讀的 Form section 卡，內容由 KV list／Stock bar／KPI 組成。右欄回答的是「改東西前我要先知道什麼」，所以放的是限制與後果（現有庫存、交付方式、這個項目掛在哪），不放正在編輯的欄位、也不放主要動作。卡片控制在 3–4 張——會捲動的右欄就不再是常駐。1100px 以下右欄會掉到主欄下方，所以裡面不能有任何「只有這條路」的任務入口。
05.2 · Pattern ▸ Voice

Task-oriented and finance-honest.以任務為導向,對財務誠實

Talks to an independent creator running their own business: plain about money, royalties, splits, and verification; never hides a fee or a pending state. Sentence case throughout. Imperative for actions, plain present for states.

對象是經營自己事業的獨立創作者:把金錢、權利金、分潤與驗證講清楚;絕不隱藏任何費用或 pending 狀態。全篇用 sentence case。動作用祈使句,狀態用平直的現在式。

Is / Is-not

該有的語氣 / 不該有的語氣

Voice is語氣是Voice is not語氣不是
Plain about money — "You'll receive $842.10 after a 12% fee"把金錢講清楚 — 「You'll receive $842.10 after a 12% fee」Vague — "Earnings will be processed"含糊 — 「Earnings will be processed」
Specific about state — "Pending until 28 Jun"把狀態講具體 — 「Pending until 28 Jun」Falsely settled — "Paid"假裝已結清 — 「Paid」
Action-first — "Request payout"動作優先 — 「Request payout」Feature-first — "Payout management module"功能優先 — 「Payout management module」
Calm, second-person — "You can edit this until the event goes live"冷靜、用第二人稱 — 「You can edit this until the event goes live」Hype / urgency — "Don't miss out!"炒作 / 製造急迫感 — 「Don't miss out!」
Honest about limits — "Bundles aren't available in your region yet"對限制誠實 — 「Bundles aren't available in your region yet」Evasive — "Coming soon" with no reason迴避 — 只說「Coming soon」卻不給原因
Conservative on compliance — "Tax docs are estimates; confirm with your advisor"合規上保守 — 「Tax docs are estimates; confirm with your advisor」Over-promising — "We handle all your taxes"過度承諾 — 「We handle all your taxes」

Microcopy

Microcopy

  • CTA primary: Create project · Request payout · Publish · Save draft
  • 主要 CTA: Create project · Request payout · Publish · Save draft
  • CTA secondary: Back · Cancel · Export CSV
  • 次要 CTA: Back · Cancel · Export CSV
  • Success: "Project saved as draft." · "Payout requested — arrives in 2–3 business days."
  • 成功: 「Project saved as draft.」(已存為草稿)· 「Payout requested — arrives in 2–3 business days.」(已申請提領,2–3 個工作天到帳)
  • Warning: "This product is referenced by 2 live projects. Editing it updates them too."
  • 警告: 「This product is referenced by 2 live projects. Editing it updates them too.」(此商品被 2 個上線中的 project 引用,編輯會一併更新它們)
  • Error: "Couldn't save. Your draft is kept — try again."
  • 錯誤: 「Couldn't save. Your draft is kept — try again.」(無法儲存,草稿已保留,請再試一次)
  • Empty (new): "No projects yet. Create your first to start earning."
  • 空白(全新): 「No projects yet. Create your first to start earning.」(還沒有 project,建立第一個就能開始賺錢)
  • Empty (filtered): "No transactions match these filters. Clear filters to see all."
  • 空白(篩選後): 「No transactions match these filters. Clear filters to see all.」(沒有交易符合這些篩選條件,清除篩選即可看全部)
  • Guidance: "Available = cleared and ready to withdraw. Pending = still in the platform's hold window."
  • 說明: 「Available = cleared and ready to withdraw. Pending = still in the platform's hold window.」(Available = 已結清可提領;Pending = 仍在平台保留期內)
  • Money state pair: "Available $842.10 · Pending $1,204.00"
  • 金額狀態組合: 「Available $842.10 · Pending $1,204.00」
  • Capitalization: sentence case for headings, paragraphs, and buttons.
  • 大小寫: 標題、段落與按鈕一律用 sentence case。
Payout requested — arrives in 2–3 business days.
This product is referenced by 2 live projects. Editing it updates them too.
Available $842.10 · Pending $1,204.00
05.3 · Pattern ▸ States & Interaction

Global interaction defaults.全域互動預設

  • Nav dropdown: hover-open with a 140ms close delay; click toggles; ESC-to-close. Panel bg uses --background.
  • Nav dropdown: hover 開啟,關閉延遲 140ms;點擊切換;按 ESC 關閉。面板背景用 --background。
  • Theme toggle: light / dark / system cycle, persisted; ?theme= one-time override.
  • Theme toggle: light / dark / system 循環,會記住;?theme= 可一次性覆寫。
  • Tabs: single active panel, URL-hash synced. Chips: single-select, result count updates on change. Switch: 150ms knob slide.
  • Tabs: 只有一個作用中面板,與 URL hash 同步。Chips: 單選,變動時更新結果數量。Switch: 150ms 滑鈕動畫。
  • Lifecycle: 404 keeps chrome + link to Dashboard; Empty stub for unbuilt routes; Error = inline Alert --row with retry, never blanks loaded data; never toast-only.
  • Lifecycle: 404 保留外框 + 提供回 Dashboard 的連結;尚未建好的路由用 Empty stub;Error = 行內 Alert --row 附重試,絕不清空已載入的資料;絕不只用 toast。
  • Motion: 150–240ms ease-out; entrance animations gated behind reduced-motion.
  • Motion: 150–240ms ease-out;進場動畫受 reduced-motion 控制。
05.4 · Pattern ▸ Data viz

Chart conventions.圖表慣例

Lives in chart.css (see §4.71). Line chart: default series --primary, comparison --muted-foreground dashed, area fill color-mix(--primary 18%). Source-breakdown palette: --primary → #000 → --status-success → --status-info → #999. Series rely on legend labels, not color alone.

放在 chart.css(見 §4.71)。折線圖:預設序列用 --primary,對照序列用 --muted-foreground 虛線,區域填色用 color-mix(--primary 18%)。來源拆解的配色:--primary → #000 → --status-success → --status-info → #999。序列靠圖例 label 區分,不只靠顏色。

Structure 把 components + patterns 組裝成頁面骨架。

Appendix A

Output formats.輸出格式

DSS v1.4 is output-agnostic. Ztor Creator Studio · R 2.1 ships as CSS Custom Properties (canonical form in ds-components/_tokens.css); below are equivalent representations for other targets.

DSS v1.4 不綁定輸出形式。Ztor Creator Studio · R 2.1 以 CSS Custom Properties 交付(canonical 形式在 ds-components/_tokens.css);以下是給其他目標的等效表示。

Code example — for developers程式碼範例 — 給工程師
:root {
  --background:         #FFFFFF;
  --card:            #FFFFFF;
  --primary:            #ffa33f;
  --primary-foreground: #171717;
  --border:             #EAEAEA;
  --status-success:     #22C55E;
}

Also expressible as Tailwind v4 @theme tokens and W3C DTCG JSON ({ "color": { "primary": { "$value": "#ffa33f", "$type": "color" } } }).

也可表示成 Tailwind v4 @theme tokens 與 W3C DTCG JSON({ "color": { "primary": { "$value": "#ffa33f", "$type": "color" } } })。

Appendix B

DSS v1.4 JSON skeleton.DSS v1.4 JSON 骨架

Code example — for developers程式碼範例 — 給工程師
{
  "record": { "name": "Ztor Creator Studio · R 2.1", "source": "Ztor Creator Studio", "version": "R 2.1" },
  "foundation": { "palette": { "orange": { "500": "#ffa33f" }, "neutral": { "50": "#FFFFFF", "900": "#171717" } } },
  "role": { "color": { "primary": { "bg": "palette.orange.500", "fg": "palette.neutral.900" } } },
  "mode": { "dark": { "color": { "bg": { "canvas": "palette.neutral.900" } } } },
  "component": { "_inventory": "button · badge · … (23 units, each with _layer)" },
  "pattern": { "_cards": { "dashboard-home": {}, "tabbed-section-view": {}, "filter-and-list": {}, "lifecycle-states": {}, "multi-step-wizard": {} } },
  "structure": "(see Pillar 6)"
}

Integrity Check

Document graph health.文件關係圖健康度

This self-check runs in the browser and validates internal anchors, duplicate IDs, compose-chip targets, and linked local CSS files. It is documentation-only and does not affect product pages.

這個自檢會在瀏覽器裡檢查內部錨點、重複 ID、compose-chip 目標，以及本地 CSS 連結。它只屬於文件，不影響產品頁。
